2a1(di): bu ye sangs 'du la be ta ha ra phyo yi sangs/ bod skad du
2a2(di): srid pa'i has zhes bya ba/ bcom ldan 'das badz+ra he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo//
2a3(di): hrIn 'di skad pa dag gis thos pa'i dris gcig na/ ring ljang god dngos bur rags
2a4(di): 'byung brjin sum ldan nga ma// gled pa me la da
2b1(di): bdag/ srid pa'i rgyal mo 'khor lo rten cing 'brel pa 'byung bas thams cad bsdus pa las/ de'i thugs
2b2(di): kha nas gos bdag chen po brgyad sprul nas 'jig rten cham la phab ste gnas pa ni/ 'di lta ste/ nA
2b3(di): po 'dzum med dang thom po yor po gnyis srid pa shar gyi skos bdag tu bskos/ skos rje drang dkar dang thod
2b4(di): ba'i 'bring ba gnyis lho'i sgos bdag tu bskos/ yam+b+ha daM ba dang yaT+Ta kro d+ha gnyis nub kyi gos bdag tu bsgos
2b5(di): 'khor lo bcu gnyis pa dang yab rje nag po gnyis byang gi skos bdag tu bskos/ de thams cad kyang badz+ra he ru
3a1(di): ka'i sku la 'khril pa'o// bdud de rnams kyis brkos gdab pas/ nam mkha' dang gling bzhi
3a2(di): rab tu bcas pas kun tu gang bas khyab pa ni/ ri rab khri 'phang bzhi pa/ bang rim dang bcas pa ni/ dpag bsam gyi
3a3(di): shing la ban pas se ba na khri/ mor dpag tshad ba ni Sh+miSh+Te/ brgyad khri ni thams cad 'gro ba rigs drug gi rten sa ste/
3a4(di): 'og gi bzhi khri ni ngan song gnas gsum mo// steng gi bzhi khri ni mtho ris kyi gnas so// gser gyi ri bdun ni rol mtsho dang
3a5(di): 'brel pas/ nam mkha' la yang mun sel gyi glog 'gyu ba'o// de la gling bzhi brten te/ gling bzhi mi bzhis rten te/
3a6(di): dbyibs mi mthun pa dang / spyod pa dang / bskyed pa dang kha dog kyang mi mthun pa ma yin no// der ri rab ni srid pa'i rgyal mo'i lto ba ste/
3b1(di): de la ni rten 'brel bcu gnyis dang / dug gsum dang / lha dang lha ma yin gyi g.yul ngo 'gyed pa dang 'gro ba rigs drug gi mi dang / byol song yi dgas dmyal ba'i gnas ni sku
3b2(di): la 'char ro// phyag gnyis ni ri rab kyi phrag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis nas 'jus zhabs gnyis ni rgya mtsho'i gting du brkyang nas gnas pa la/ ri rab kyang 'gul/
3b3(di): gling bzhi yang ldeg/ rgya mtsho yang 'khrug pa las/ 'jig rten stongs la khad nas/ badz+ra he ru ka'i dgongs pas 'di la ting nge 'dzin gyi gzer cig ma btab na/
3b4(di): 'jig rten stongs par dgongs nas/ zil gnon gyi phyag rgya dang bcas nas/ sku lte ba man chud bsnun te mo'i b+ha ga la bslab par byas so// der ri rab kyi zur bzhin
3b5(di): lcog chen po bzhi gnas pa la/ khang pa brtsegs pa bzhin ded dpon chen po bzhi gnas so// lha'i ded dpon ni 'khor lo bcu gnyis pa/ ba dan dkar po bsnams pa/
3b6(di): shel khrab dang shel rmog gsol ba/ chibs su ba glang dkar po gser gyi snal chu la dar gyi sna thag can bcings pa'o// lha bran dar cha can bdun bdun gyi g.yog byas pa'o//
3b7(di): lha ma yin gyi ded dpon ni bse khrab dang bse rmog gsol pa/ lha ma yin gyi g.yog bdun gyis bskor ba ber nag can bdun no// bdud dang gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon ni zangs kyi
4a1(di): 'phar ba la non pa/ stod zangs la smad lcags kyi khrab can lcags rmog gsol ba/ 'khor mang pos bskor ba/ 'khor rnams dmar nag tu 'dug
4a2(di): pas bskor ba'o// ma mo'i dad dponi na sku la g.yu khra ba dang gsu rmog gsol ba/ dar nag lce lnga pa'i ba dan bsnams pa/ zangs kyi ma mo ske rings la zhon pa/ byang shar na gnas
4a3(di): pas so so'i nas 'dul lo// lha ma yin ni dbang dkar po lce dmar po'o// bdud dang gnod sbyin ni dar sna lnga'i ba dan no// lkog gi rtse mo la rgyal mtshan bzhi re re gnas so// stag dang /
4a4(di): gzig dang / bya rgod dang / rma bya'i rgyal mtshan gnas so// de ni dga' ba'i tshal la sogs pa'o// tshal bzhi ni 'dres pa'i tshul du gnas pa'o// da na ni shing yongs su
4a5(di): sa brtol gnas te yon tan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'o// de na ma srid pa'i rgyal mo la badz+ra he ru ka sa brgyan pa la/ gnal yas khang ni gser gyi 'khor lo 'od dang 'bar ba lte ba
4a6(di): kha dog sna tshogs mdzes pas brgyan la/ mu khyud dkar po dang gru chad ljang khu/ bar khyams ni shar dkar po/ lho bai DUR+Ya sngon po/ nub rA ga dmar po/ byang
4a7(di): iN+Din la ljang khu/ de'i phyi rim na sgo snam dang sga khyud drag pa lcags kyis byas pa/ gru gsum gsum brtsegs ni nag po dmar po ser po'o// yon tan sna
4b1(di): tshogs dang ldan pa gser gyi 'khor lo bya'o// de ni rgyu mched kyis nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'o// thod pa skam rlon gyi rtsig pas brtan par byas la/ de thams
4b2(di): cad khrag gi zham chu 'bab pa/ dur khrod kyi lce spyang sang po khrag la brjod cing 'thung ba/ keng rus dang sha khrag mang po ri rab tsam du spungs pa/ zhing chen gyi rgyal mtshan dang / 'phan
4b3(di): gdugs dang / bla re bres pa/ kang ka la sogs te dur bya'i tshogs mang po lding ba/ gnod sbyin pho mo mang po 'dub/ nyi zla'i mthong khung dang / gza' chen po brgyad kyi
4b4(di): ka gzhu dang / zhing stug po'i ka ba dang / dar nag gi ldi lnga dang / phel kha che chung dang / mchog phran gyi dral phye ma dang / rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa'i gnas na/ bcom ldan 'das badz+ra
4b5(di): he ru ka dang yum srid pa'i rgyal mo la/ gnod sbyin pha mo mang pos bskor ba ni/ 'di lta ste/ dbyings yum drug la/ bde ba che snyoms ma yid kyi rtsa las bskyed pa dang / yid 'ong
4b6(di): rgyal mo ba ga las sems kyi rtsa las bskyed pa dang / 'khor lo tshim byed mnyon mongs pa'i rtsa las bskyed pa dang / 'gro ba sgrol byed ma mkha' lding gi rtsa las bskyed pa dang / thos
4b7(di): byed kyi rtsa las yid 'phrog ma bskyed pa dang snum byed kyi rtsa las chags byed rgyal mo bskyed pa dang drug ni dbyings kyi yum drug ces bya'o// yum drug ces bya ba ni
5a1(di): ma mo thams cad de drug la bskyed pas yum drug ces bya'o// srid pa bde 'gro ma bde ba cha snyoms ma'i yid las bskyed pas/ rtag tu 'khor lo dang
5a2(di): ba na d+ha bsnams pa'o// yid 'ong rgyal mo'i sems las rnam snang gsal bskyed pas/ 'byung ba nam mkha' la dbang byed do// 'khor lo tshom byed ma'i nyon mongs pa'i rtsa las
5a3(di): bkra gsal 'bar bskyed pas/ 'byung ba sa la dbang sgyur ba dang / 'gro ba sgrol byed ma'i mig gi rnam par shes pa las 'od gsal 'bar bskyed pas/ 'byung ba me la dbang sgyur ba'o//
5a4(di): yid 'phrog ma'i rna ba'i rnam shes las gnyen gsal 'bar bskyed pa las/ 'byung ba chu la dbang bsgyur ba dang / chags byed rgyal mo'i sna'i rnam par shes pa las g.yang gsal g.yos
5a5(di): bskyed pas/ 'byung ba rlung la dbang sgyur ba'o// de yang dpyid kyi yum drug la dpal chen pos dbang ming gis bskur ba ni/ dga' ba'i me tog mangs ldan ma zhes bde ba cha snyoms
5a6(di): ma la dbang bskur ro// yid 'ong ma la rin chen lcug ma zhes bya'o// 'khor tshim byed ma la 'bar ma 'od chags ma zhes dbang bskur ro// 'gro ba sgrol byed ma la ri rab brjid ldan ma
5a7(di): zhes dbang bskur ro// yid 'phrog ma la 'khor ba chags pas tshim mdzad ma zhes btags/ chags byed rgyal mo kun skyod ma zhes ming gis dbang bskur ro// dbyings kyi yum
5b1(di): drug mo de ni dbu gsum gsum ste/ dga' ba'i me tog ma zhal dbus ser/ g.yas dkar/ g.yon ljang nag go/ rin chen lcug ma'i dbus sngo/ g.yas ser/ g.yon
5b2(di): dmar 'brar ba'i 'od chags ma'i zhal dbus rA ga/ g.yas mthing ka/ g.yon dmar/ ri rab brjid ldan ma la dbus dkar/ g.yas ser/ g.yon dmar ro// 'khor ba
5b3(di): chags pas tshim mdzad ma ni zhal dbus ldang / g.yas dmar/ g.yon dkar/ chags byed rgyal mo ni zhal dbus ser/ g.yas nag/ g.yon mthing ka'i zhal/ de drug ka'i g.yas
5b4(di): dang po drug na ban d+ha khrag gis bkang ba bsnams pa'o// g.yon gyi dang po kun na dang nag gi ru mtshon byar ba'o// bar ma dang tha ma na sna tshogs kyi mtshon cha phyar ba'o// rtag pa'i rgyal
5b5(di): mo drug kyang dbu gsum gsum mo// phyag mtshan sku mdog kun gzhung dang mthun no// rtag pa'i rgyal mo drug ni rnam snang gsal ni 'gro ba'i sems la dbang sgyur/ bkra gsal 'bar
5b6(di): ni 'gro ba'i shal dbang sgyur/ gnyen gsal 'bar ni 'gro ba'i khrag la dbang sgyur/ 'od gsal 'bar ni 'gro ba'i drod la dbang sgyur/ g.yang gsal g.yos ni 'gro ba'i dbugs la dbang sgyur//
5b7(di): srid pa bde 'gro ni 'gro ba'i mdangs la sbyar ro// bskyed pa'i khro mo bcu gsum po phyir mi 'ong gi spun drug yin/ zhes gtso mo dang bcu gsum pa la bya'o// de rnams ni gtso mo'i 'khor ro// de
6a1(di): nas bang rim dang po la ni rnal 'byor ma bzhi khros pa'i dbang chen bzhi phung byed sbas pa'i ma bzhi dang / nyi zla stong gi thod 'phreng dang / 'phra men rgya mtsho'i rnam
6a2(di): ni dbu gsum gsum mo// gzhan zhal gcig phyag gnyis so// nyi zla stong gi thod 'phreng ni zhal dbus dkar/ g.yon sngo/ g.yas ser ro// phyag drug gi dang po na thod pa khrag gis
6a3(di): bkang ba bsnams/ bar ma na gser gyi 'khor lo tha ma na g.yu'i ga'u/ phyag g.yon dang po ni nyi zla/ ba ra ma na g.yu'i khra/ tha ma na rgyu ma'i zhags pa bsnams pa'o// 'phra men rgya
6a4(di): mtsho dbus sna tshogs kyi zhal/ g.yas dkar/ g.yon dmar/ phyag g.yas dang po na puSh+pe dkar po khrag gis bkang ba/ ba rA ma na zhing gi ru mtshon/ tha ma nA ne'u le'i rgyal ba/
6a5(di): g.yon dang bin ti ra'i dbyug pa/ ba ra ba na sbrul nag gi ru mtshon/ tha man lcags kyu bsdams pa'o// de ni rnal 'byol ma bcu'i 'khor ro// srid pa sman mo'i 'khor nI/ mam
6a6(di): bdun dang / sring mo bzhi dang / rgyas 'debs bzhi dang / dmag gi rgyal mo bzhi dang / i ka dza ti spun drug dang / gru 'debs bzhi dang / bya ba mo dang / byed pa mo gnyis dang /
6a7(di): dbang phyug ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang / de ltar shar gyi dkar mo bum thogs ma shel gyi khang pan gnas pas/ de'i khri 'phang yar 'phags mar nub pa'i rtsa na gnas so// ljon sngon ma
6b1(di): bubrumum thogs ma bzhi bai DUR+Ya'i khang pa na gnas so// nub na dmar mo byu ru'i bum pa thogs pa bzhi gnas so// byung na ser mo gser gyi bum pa thogs pa bzhi gnas te/ phyogs bzhi'i
6b2(di): sring mo bzhi bzhi yin/ tshe'i lha mo bcu drug ces kyang de la bya'o// lcags ri mu khyud 'das pa'i pha rol na/ mun pa'i g.yung drung gling bar gyi mun pa'i nang shes na/ zor bdag chen mo bzhi
6b3(di): ni dga' mo gnyen gyi zor 'phen ma/ ar+g+ha gnyen gyi sman cig ma// rag+na gnyen gyi tsa mun tri// dre'u gdong chen mo mgo gcod ma// zhes thams cad kyi las la shis pa'i mam
6b4(di): bzhi'o// nam mkha' stong pa la dbang sgyur ba'i ma ma ni/ bdud kyi ma mo nag mo dung mgrin ma dang / sa bdag dang klu la dbang sgyur ba g.yu'i bye'u can gyi 'khor gyis bskor ni/ ma mo
6b5(di): brgya rtsa brgyad kyi khung nas brgyud pa'o// de las spros na stong rtsa brgyad du 'gyur ba'o// de yang ma mo rigs bzhir bsdus pa las/ dbyings kyi ma mo gtso mo srid pa'i rgyal mo dang / bung
6b6(di): byed sbas pa'i ma mo bzhi dang / bskyed pa'i khro mo bcu gsum la sogs pa ni dbyings kyi ma mo'o// bdud mo kun gyi gtso ma ni e ka dza ti dang / rnal 'byor nyid dbyings bcu bzhi dang / nag mo dung
6b7(di): mgrin la sogs pa ni bdud mo'i rigs so// yang gab ma bzhi dang / g.yu'i bye'u can dang / tsha ba mgau ti bdag mo mgo dgu ral gcig ma dang / ro ba shal ma dang / dra me dra dang / rma
7a1(di): ri chen mo la sogs pa ni sprul pa'i ma mo'i rigs so// gtso mo gdug byed nag mo dang / bse ba ti'i bdag mo dang / gdong mo bzhi dang / dur khrod
7a2(di): kyi bdag mo shri tsa mun tri dang / rgya ri skye ser kha 'a ba ra rka na sgra can la sogs pa ni las byed ma'i rigs so// 'dren cing 'gugs pa'i las byed pa/ ny+tsal le nyis brgya lnga bcu gnyis
7a3(di): mngag cing gzhu pa'i las byed pa// pho nya nyis brgya lnga bcu gnyis// gsod cing gcod pa'i las byed pa// bdud mo nyis brgya lnga bcu gnyis// 'gugs shing 'dren
7a4(di): pa'i las byed pa// sman phran nyis brgya lnga bcu gnyis// ma mo stong dang brgyad du grags// bsdus na dbyings kyi ma mor 'dus// kun kyang gtso mo yum du 'dus// gtso mo yun
7a5(di): yang dkyil 'khor chen por 'dus// dang por bskyed pa hUM du 'dus// hUM yang thig le chos skur 'dus// ma ni chos kyi dbyings yin te// mo ni rig pa'i ye shes yin//
7a6(di): chos kyi sku ru thams cad rdzogs// zhes gsungs so// ma mo srid pa'i bems las/ gleng gzhi'i skabs te dang po'o// // de nas g.yung drung
7a7(di): gis 'di skad ces gsol to// yab cig 'jig rten 'joms pa'i lha// skos bdag rgyal po ji ltar lags// srid pa cha ma la ji ltar dbab// yab cig bdag la bka' stsol
7b1(di): cig/ ces gsol pas bka' stsal pa/ skos rje drang dkar la sogs brgyad// srid pa b+h+yo bzlog mdos kyi skos// shar lho nub byang phyogs bzhi nas// 'dod pa'i ma
7b2(di): mo'i rdzas rnams skos kyi 'grem// bka' blo na bsgo ba thams cad byed// ma mo rnams kyi mngag gzhug yin// srid pa cha ma la dbab pa ni// lha min g.yul ngo bzlog pa ste//
7b3(di): srid pa'i ri rab bcas nas ni// steng du srid pa'i rgyal mo bzhi// gzhung dang 'thun par dbyung bar bya// dbyings kyi yum drung gzhung bzhin bri// yang na gsang phye dag la bya//
7b4(di): smug nag sngo nag ljang nag drug/ gzhung dang 'thun par bri bar bya// de nas skang rdzas bsags pa ni// gzugs mdzes bri 'am 'bur du dgod// mkha' lding rgyal po shang shang
7b5(di): drug/ rigs dang kha dog mtshungs par bya// khyung chen drug dang mdangs ldan rma bya drug/ de bzhin mdzes pa'i btsun mo drug/ go dor drug dang skyes pa drug/ rigs dang mthun par
7b6(di): bris pa drug/ sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan nas kyang // btsun mo drug ni khyung la bskyon// skyes pa drug ni go dor la// stag gzig chas su bcug la bskyon// rgyal po drug/
7b7(di): ni 'khor dang bcas// 'gying bag bcas te glang chen drug la bskyon// dbyings kyi yum la dbul bar bya// shing ris drug ni sna tshogs mdzes par tshon gyis byug/ rigs
8a1(di): dang bstun te mdzes par bya// gnyis la ri dgas rgyal po sha ba drug/ bud med drug kyang bri bar bya// bya dang sna tshogs che ba'i nyi zla bri// mkha
8a2(di): thabs sgo bsrungs blon po drug kyang bri// khu byug gsung snyan drug dang dpag bsam shing lor ldan// mdzes pa'i stag so ya tha yin// sna tshogs dar las tshom bu drug
8a3(di): drug pa'i rgyang bu drug/ ring thung lus kyi tshad du bya// rma bya sgro yi mdangs kyis brgyan// mo 'phang rigs dang mthun pa drug/ sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan par bya// gtso ma'i
8a4(di): nam mkha' kun du zhal// drug la khong pa nag po ste// ser po sngon po dkar po dmar// sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan nas kyang // rma bya sgro yis brgyan par bya// mdzes pa'i yun
8a5(di): la dbul bya// 'di la 'di rnams gsungs te/ 'khor na gnas pa'i ma mo gsum gsum po la nam mkha' nag mo gser gyi kha cag can bco brgyad la ras ma sngon dmar dang rgod
8a6(di): kyi bod kyis rgyan pa btang ngo // ma mo kha blo na re/ gung blon re/ nang blon re'o// nam mkha'i dbyings phyug ma dang / 'byung ba'i bcud 'byin ma dang / mkha' la gar ting shag dang / dus
8a7(di): gsum du rgyu ba'i glog 'phreng can dang / ha ra ti nag mo dang / dun ting sngon mo dang / me za brag gyon ma dang / me tog mdangs kyi rgyal mo dang / srid pa'i g.yul ngo zlog byed ma
8b1(di): dang / 'od ldan rgyal mo dang / nyi ma'i 'od zer can dang / 'od chags g.yu'i ral gcig ma dang / dung thod thig le can dang / rdo rje bya mgo ma dang / kha na me 'bar ma dang / ri rab
8b2(di): rdo rje bskur ma dang / 'khor lo dri zhon ma dang / e ma'ur sgra can dang / bco brgyad po de ni kha blon dang / gung blon dang / nang blon dang / de rnams la ngar glud mdzub gang ba re
8b3(di): chas su bcug la dbul bar bya'o// 'phang sna tshogs pa re nam mkha' bzhin brgyan pa dbul bar bya'o// de rnams ni dbyings kyi yum drug gi 'khor dang bcas pa'i chas su 'debs
8b4(di): pa'o// da ni rtag pa'i rgyal me drug la bsngo ba ni/ seng ge g.yu'i rang sa na drug/ ba glang dkar po gser gyi sna chu can drug la/ skyes pa chas su bcug pa
8b5(di): bcu drug bskyon pa dang / khyung drug la dar snas brgyan pa dang / rta drug la btsun mo gu zu can chas su bcug pa bcu drug dang / me mo mdzes ma drug la gser g.yus brgyan pa drug
8b6(di): po ni phyir kha bltas pa'i bang rim dang por dgod/ 'bru sna lnga la rin po che sna lnga btang / spos dang sha bal btang / bse 'gron bu lung tang zangs ma lcags de rnams la ngar glud
8b7(di): khru gang ba cig byas la/ bza' mi du yod pa'i ming 'o ma dang mtshal sbyar la bris la rus kyang gzhug/ mgo la g.yu gdags lag tu nor phyugs dang / zangs lcags dang
9a1(di): 'bru'i bag dang / shog gu la bris la ci yod pa'i rdzas bskur/ gos dang rgyun sna tshogs gdags so// de nas shing ris 'phan bzang drug la
9a2(di): rdo rje dang pad+ma rin po che 'khor lo rgya gra ma ral gri bri/ khyung re re/ rma bya re re/ ne tso gsung snyan re re/ shing lo'i kha nas skad snyan po sgrog pa re re bri/ ba da na lce lnga pa re re bri/ ri
9a3(di): dgas rgyal mo drug bri/ nyi zla 'og nas 'char ba bri/ mda' ris dang bstun pa drug bri/ nam mkha' kha dog rigs dang bsnun pa la mdzes tshon du byas pa drug bri/ 'phang
9a4(di): drug gi kha dog mthun/ rma byas kun rgyan dar sna tshogs dang bzang sgros brgyan/ khams gsum yum mchog la rgod kyi ldem ru gzugs/ rgyang bu drug lus tshad du bya/
9a5(di): dar gyi tshom bu gsum gsum gdags so// 'bru bya tshang ba ni g.yog mo rnams la bsngo/ ting lo mar gyis bkang ba bco brgyad sdong bu dang bcas pa bya'o// ngar glud chags gang
9a6(di): ba drug bya/ gos su bskon no// ma chos kyi rgyan gcig ma dang / thor tshugs gcig ma dang / keng rus thod 'phreng can dang / dbugs bdag ral gcig ma dang / nag mo
9a7(di): mchu 'phyangs ma dang / smag nag mig gsum ma dang / dkar mo zhi ba'i 'od 'phro ma dang / nag mo chen mo mgyogs ma rlung zhon ma dang / smug nag chen mo ti ra'i ro rkun ma dang /
9b1(di): dmar po 'od chags ral gcig ma dang / ser mo sbrul gyi gshog pa can dang / sa bdag chen mo bse'i ral pa can dang / bdud rtsi dmar mo dang / smug nag chen mo mgo dgu ma
9b2(di): dang gtum mo chen mo mgo dag ma dang / lag 'thung spyan gcig ma dang / re mkhar nag mo dang / rgya nad gtong ba'i ma mo dred gdong ma dang / bco brgyad po de ni 'khor 'dul/
9b3(di): tshi mo zhes bya'o// da ni rnal 'byor ma bcu gnyis kyi bskang rdzas bstan te/ gtso mo gnyis la sgro'i bskang ba'i rdzas rnams ni/ khrung khrung dkar me la
9b4(di): dar za 'og go zu can btsun mo chas su bcug pa dang / 'phra men rgya mtsho la gzig chas can skyes pa stag chas can bskyon par bya/ gzhan ni spyi'i bskang rdzas su stag bcu bzhi/ gzig bcu bzhi/ khyi
9b5(di): dkar po gser gyi yang chung can bcu bzhi/ khyung bcu bzhi/ rma bya bcu bzhi/ shang shang bcu bzhi/ gzhan yang sa'i 'bras bu ku lan ta/ sha sna tshang ba'i gtor ma bzhi/ stag
9b6(di): chas gzig chas dar thasa' bzangs gser g.yu go mtshon dang / mi la yod pa'i rdzas kun 'tshogs tshad du bsogs/ de nas mda' gzhung dang 'thun pa bcu bzhi/ shing ris lnga de yang
9b7(di): gtso mo gnyis la re re/ khros pa'i dbang chen bzhi la gcig/ thugs kyi dgyes sde mo bzhi la gcig/ 'phung byed sbas pa'i ma bzhi la gcig/ mda' yang rgyas par byed na
10a1(di): bcubasdu na lnga/ gzhung dang mthun par bcu bzhi bri// 'phang ni lnga ru bsdu bar bya// nam mkha' rgyang bu bcu bzhi'o// nyi zla thod 'phreng
10a2(di): la khor dkar mo la mdzes pa'i tshon du bris pa'o// 'phra men gyi rma bzang ma la dar gyi spyang lag gtso mo gnyis la dgod/ rma bya'i mdongs kyis brgyan par bya/ khros
10a3(di): pa'i dbang chen bzhi la khong nag mo la gser gyi kha cag bzhi/ dgyes sde bzhi la g.yu'i khong pa la phyi rim gser la kha cha ga dung / ma mo bzhi la gcig khong pa gser la phyi rim
10a4(di): g.yugacig khong pa gnag la phyi rim gser/ gcig khong pa g.yul phyi rim dung / gcig ni khong pa g.yul phyi rim nag/ kha chag bye rus byas pa yin// 'phang lnga
10a5(di): rgyan dang bcas pa yis// de ni 'khor na gnas pa la// bal tshon rgyang bu gsum pa sbyin// kun kyang ring thung lus kyi tshad// nam mkha' rgyang bu sna tshogs re re sbyin//
10a6(di): sna tshogs ras ma sgo yis brnyan// 'khor na gnas pa'i mamo bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis 'di rtso / sngon mo khro gnyer sbrul nag can/ ma btsun mthing gi sgro mo dang sgrol
10a7(di): byed lcags kyu can dang / dre'u gdong 'khor lo can dang / btsan gyi bu mo dan ting shig dang / gza'i bu mo thogs 'phen ma dang / bdud kyi bu mo mog gcig ma dang /
10b1(di): kha la me 'bar ri rab 'phen dang / tshangs pa gzi can gyi bu mo gzi brjid 'od ldan ma dang / mun pa'i bu mo rkang gcig dang / gnod sbyin gyi bu mo rab 'bar sla bo che dang / klu'i bu mo
10b2(di): de ring mo dang / rab 'bar spra bo che dang / nag mo bya rog gi gdong ba can dang / thal mdog khro gnyer can dang / re ma ti dang / gser gyi 'bru gcig ma dang / ar+ya gnyen gyi
10b3(di): ma ti dang / keng rus chen mo g.yag mgo can dang / nag mo sbrul mgo can dang / nag mo bse gdong mig gcig ma dang / klu'i bu mo g.yu'i lan tshar can yid 'ong dge dang / mtsho
10b4(di): sman gyi rgyal mo sbrul nag gi gu zu can dang / ral gcig rgya mtsho dang / dpag bsam nam gru ma dang / bdud 'dul dbang gi lha mo dang / dpal lha mo nag mo dang / bya thul can dang /
10b5(di): thugs kyi gzer chen dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi dpal mo can dang sa'i ma mo khrag nad gtong ba dang / bar snang khams la brgyal nad gtong ma dang / nam mkha'i mthongs nas
10b6(di): mkhris pa sha ya dang / bal nad 'dar bu gtong ba 'ong / mtsho sman chen mo dkar mo dbu dgu ma dang / smug mo dbu lnga ma dang / rag+na tsa mun ti dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi dkar
10b7(di): mo g.yu'i thong rdeng can dang / rnam sman dkar mo nyi 'od 'bar ba'i sman gcig mas so// srid pa gsum gyi thod rdeng can dang / rmir rab 'byam rdo rje grags mo rgyal lo// de ltar ma
11a1(di): mo bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis ni rnal 'byor ma bcu bzhi'i 'khor na gnas pas de la mchod par bya'o// de man chad na srid pa'i sman mo lnga bcu rtsa dgu gnas
11a2(di): te/ ma mo bdun la ni/ nam ma kha'i nag mo dung gi kha cag can/ bdun bya spu dang ra sa ma sna tshogs kyis brgyan te/ 'phang nag mo bdun la gser gyi me long rtsal ba dang rgyang bu bdun
11a3(di): no// mda' nag mo bdun la/ gzi ris gnyis/ stag so ris gnyis chu mig ris gnyis/ mkhar thabs zo ba'iris ni gtso mo lnga la bsgo'o// sring mo bzhi la phyogs
11a4(di): dang bstun pa'i nam mkha' bzhi sor bzhi mdzes pa'i kha dog gdab par bya'o// mda' ni dkar dmar dang ni ser dang sngo// thig le stagaso ldan par bri// nyi zla sman mo kun gyi gong nas
11a5(di): 'char/ ma mo'i grangs ni ji bzhin rgyang bu bya// shing ris ma mo bdun la gcig/ sring mo bzhi la gcig/ 'phang yang de bzhin grub tshad bya// gru 'degs bzhi la shing ris
11a6(di): gcig/ dmag gi rgyal mo bzhi la shing ris gcig/ gsang ba'i yum chen bzhi la shing ris gcig/ rgyang bu re re gcad pa min// gsang ba'i yum bzhi la/ nam mkha' khong pa
11a7(di): dkar po 'ja' ris bzhi ka la/ mdzes pa'i tshon gyis bri bar bya// mda' yang phyogs kyis bsgyur ba la// shar du dkar mo stag so ris// lho ru sngon mo gzi ris bri// nub
11b1(di): tu dmar mo zo ba kha sprod bri// byang du ser mo nya mig dgod// dmag gi rgyal mo bzhi la yang // kha dog nag mo bsgyur ba la// dkar mo ri mo gsum gsum dang / ser po dmar po
11b2(di): gsum pa bri// e ka dza Ti spun drug la g.yu yi kha chag btang // mda' ni gzhung dang mthun par bri// shing ris gcig la sna tshogs ldan par bya// stag so nyi zla'i gong du bya'o//
11b3(di): rgyang bu shing ris lus tshad bgyi// gru ldegs chen mo bzhi po la// re'u dang 'bre'u'i nam mkha' dang // zangs ma dmar mo ser mo bya// stag gzig bris pa'i shing ris bya
11b4(di): bya ba mo dang byed pa mo gnyis// thams cad kyi bdag nyid yin pas// shing ris lus tshad gnyis bya ste// gcig la dpag pas ma shing du bris// yal ga re la bkra shis
11b5(di): kyi bya mdzes par skad snyan sna tshogs bri nyi zla gnyis ni 'og nas 'char/ gong na kha yal lel dang gsang phye phyo bya ba/ logs la ni ri dgas mig bzhi rgyu ba/ tshon sna sna tshogs
11b6(di): kyis mdzes par bris la/ dar sna mang po'i spyang lag gdags so// gcig la kha yal yel dang gsang phye phye'i 'og tu khyung kha sprod gnyis/ de'i 'og tu btsun mo chas bzang
11b7(di): ma gnyis bri/ de'i 'og tu ri dgas grub tshad bri/ de gnyis ri rab kyi steng du srid pa'i rgyal mo'i mdun rgyab tu gzugs so// sman mo thams cad la srog chags ni gnam la lding
12a1(di): dgu dang / sa la 'dzul dgu'i gzugs grub tshad du bya'o// spyan gzigs kyi gtor ma bzhi phyogs bzhir bzhag go/ srid pa'i bems las le'u ste
12a2(di): gnyis pa'o// // de nas lha g.yung drung gis 'di skad ces gsol to// kye ma ho yab cig 'jig rten 'joms mdzad lha// srid pa b+h+yo ldog mdos 'di
12a3(di): la/ ri rab gling bzhi ji ltar bca'// skus bdag brgyad kyi glung ni gang // yab kyis bdag la bka' stsol cig/ ces de nyid na 'khod do// yab kyis bka' stsal pa/
12a4(di): rgyu ni gsang phye srang phyed la// cha gcig ri rab gling bzhi bca'// rin chen sna lnga btang bar bya// 'o ma spos dang chu gtsang gis// legs par brdzis te khri 'phang bzhi ru brtsigs//
12a5(di): steng du zur bzhi la cog bzhi'i steng du// ded dpon bzhi gzhung dang 'thun par gzugs su dgod// steng du srid pa'i rgyal mo'i zhal// mngon du gzhung dang mthun par dbyung //
12a6(di): gling phran rnams ni legs par bca'// 'dzam bu gling ni sngon po la// mi rnams 'dra ba'i gzugs gsum bya// gos dang kha dog 'di 'dra'i chas su bya// shar ni dkar po yin
12a7(di): pa ste// mi yi dbyibs kyang zla kham tshul// bong che kha dog dkar por bya// byang dang lho yang de bzhin te// mi ni gsum gsum kun nas chas kyis mdzes par brgyan//
12b1(di): shar gyi gsum po shar gyi sgos bdag la// dmar gtor re dang bcas te dbul// lho dang nub dang byad kyang de bzhin no// dang po dbyings kyi yum drug dgod// de yang
12b2(di): gsang phye phul bzhi la// yum drug sku ni che bar bya// yang na shog shog dag la tshon gyis legs par bri// thams cad bang rim dang po la// 'khor dang bcas pa dgod
12b3(di): par bya// de nas rtag pa'i rgyal mo drug/ de nas gsang phye bre phyed la// sku gzugs yang ni shog bu la// mdzes pa'i gzugs ldan dbul bar bya// btsun mo mdzes
12b4(di): pa drug dang mdzes pa'i rdzas rnams dgod// gtso mo yum la dar sna lnga yi gur yang dbub// rgyal mo drug la mthing nag gur yang dbub// yum chen drug la 'ja' tshon khang
12b5(di): pa dbug/ de nas 'phra men rgya mtsho dang // nyi zla thod 'phreng gnyis la che bar bya// rdul 'byor bcu gnyis chung bar bya// gsang phye bre gang dag la bya// yang na shog pu
12b6(di): dag la bri// 'thun pa'i rdzas rnams bsogs par bya// bang rim gsum pa dag la dgod// bzhi pa srid pa'i sman mo'i tshogs// sna tshogs 'thun rdzas bsogs par
12b7(di): bya// gzhan yang spyi yi bskang rdzas ni// sha chen gtor ma cha bzhi bsham// phyogs bzhir khrag gis bkang la bzhag/ ri rab steng gi rgyal mo bdun// sna
13a1(di): tshogs sha sna'i gtor ma la// phud dang bdud rtsi sman gyis dgang // snang ba'i mar me gtams par bya// rgyal mo nyid kyi mthun rdzas yin//
13a2(di): rtag pa'i rgyal mo drug la yang // spyan gzigs gtor ma cha gcig dang // phud dang sman gyis mchod par bya// yum chen drug la bskang ba ni// sha chen gtor ma cha
13a3(di): gcig dang // sna tshogs snying sna'i 'phreng ba gdags// 'ja' tshon khang pa phud dang mar mer bcas// 'thun pa'i rdzas su dbul bar bya// rnal 'byor chen mo bcu bzhi
13a4(di): la// rak+ta gtor ma sman dang phud// sha chen gtor mchil chen dang // s+pha ra ma ti'i mchod pa 'bul// sman mo rnams la dbul ba ni// tshogs dang mar me zhal
13a5(di): zas dang // nag smug rdzas kyis thugs dam ba skang // spyi yi rdzas rnams bstan pa ni// rdza rnga cang te'u gling bu dang // rdza rnga sil snyan sna tshogs yang // 'phan
13a6(di): dang gdugs kyang dbul bar bya// skam chas thams cad bdag la g.yog/ mda' dang 'phang dang nam mkha' yang // dbyar dgun cha yis rab tu brgyan//
13a7(di): shing ris kun kyang dar gyi chas// tshe yi lha mo bcu drug la// tshe yi bum pa bug rdol med pa ru// bdud rtsi dza gad blug nas ni// be rgyam dkar phro ma gzhag par
13b1(di): bya/ snying po lnga yang nang du blug/ de nas phyogs bzhir gdan gyi steng du bzhag/ bu mo gtsang ma chas su bcu pa bzhi// mda' dar me long bzhi thogs la// tshe
13b2(di): yi snying po 'bod du gzhug/ phyogs bzhir nam mkha' bzhi bzhi dbul// phud gtsang gtor zhing gtor ma btang // zor bdag chen mo bzhi yi rdzas// nam mkha' nag mo gser
13b3(di): gyi kha cag can lho/ nam mkha' ser mo dung gi kha cag can shar/ dmar mo g.yu'i kha cag can nub sngon me byu ru'i kha cag can byang / seng ldeng phur bu shar
13b4(di): mchog phur byang / skyer bur lho/ zangs phur nub 'khor rang gi gzugs ci 'dra ba ba ni dgod/ lcags ri 'das pa'i pha rol na gru gsum bzhi la dgod do// de
13b5(di): nas skyes pa chas su bcug pa bzhi/ 'phar ba 'am spyang khu la bskyon la glud du 'bul lo// shog bu la bris na rab/ ded dpon bzhi la kho rang ji bzhin dbu la/ bya
13b6(di): khra kha dog so so dang mthun pa bzhi dang dmag mi bdun bdun mdzes par bris la dbul bar bya/ de nas slob dpon chas gos dang ldan par bya ba ni/ dar nag gi ber go na/ re
13b7(di): ba nag mo'i lham gon/ thod nag pos bcings/ dpral bar rgya long mtheb gang ba gdag sa/ rgya ba dang mdun du dar dkar gyis snying nan btang / me long snying khar
14a1(di): gdags so// rta mgrin nam dpal chen po'i ting nge 'dzin du zhugs la gyer gzugs so// rtag pa'i rgyal mo man chad gyer kun mthun no//
14a2(di): skos bdag brgyad dang / dbyings kyi yum drug dang / srid pa'i g.yul ngo bzlog pa'i ded dpon bzhi/ zor bdag mo bzhi ba skang lugs mi gcig pas nan tan rgyal mo
14a3(di): sa bya'o// gtso mo bcos na kun kyang bde nas gsus so// des na gtso mo'i rdzas dang bskyed pa'i mamo bcu gnyis pa'i rjes mtshogs na mi rung ngo // ma mo sring
14a4(di): pa'i bems chen po las/ srid pa b+h+yo bzlog gi mdos chen mo rdzogs so// gtan la phab pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas yang lha ga yung drung
14a5(di): gis 'di skad ces gsol to// dpa' bo 'jig rten 'joms pa'i lha// rnal 'byor nad kyis thebs gyur na// ma mo gang dang gang gi bka' chad lags// 'jig rten
14a6(di): 'joms mdzad bka' stsol cig/ ces de nyid na 'khod do// 'jig rten 'joms pas bka' stsal pa// nyon cig g.yung drung lha yi gtso// nga yis 'di ltar
14a7(di): bstan pa yin// lci zhing 'thibs na yig 'gags// gtso mo yum gyi bka' chad lags// brgyal zhing so tshigs lce ril byed// dbyings kyi yum drug bka'
14b1(di): chad yin// ro stong brang du gzer bas snying mi dga'// smug mo lcags bral bka' chad yin// mig ser za 'phrug bzhin rnams sngo// yang dag ba ma bzhi'i bka
14b2(di): chad yin// smad mi bde zhing rkang pa brid// zla lto che zhing zhim dang che// rgyal mo lnga yi bka' chad yin// gnogs byed na ning bzhin log pa// kha zas
14b3(di): yid gar mi 'ong na// phung byed ma bzhi'i bka' chad yin// mgo gzir drag la tshul zhing ni// nyi zla thod 'phreng bcos par bya// 'dar zhing rngam pa drag po 'ong /
14b4(di): ma mo bdun la mchod par bya// brang rgyab sbyar na drag po chags// yi ga mi bde stong sgrags byed// e ka spun drug bcos par bya// 'tshig cing smra ning ngu ning
14b5(di): 'bros// smug mo lcam dral bcos par bya// pho stod bcos la sham skye// rgyu ba ngan pa nyal snying 'dod// zas kyang mi zhim mdog kyang gnag/ 'di rnams bcos
14b6(di): pa'i ma mo ni// shriHtsa mun ched du bcos// spyir ni bdud mo'i rigs ka bcos// lus po lci la rkang lag 'dar// khong pa spo 'a khrog byed pa na// lha mo nag po
14b7(di): bcos par bya// spyir yang bdud mo'i rigs ka bcos// yar la skyug cing mar la 'byung // so dreg 'chags shing dang ka bde// rgya re skye ser bcos par bya/
15a1(di): khong pa na zhing gsus pa rdzis// mtsho sman mched lnga bcos par bya// smad tshigs na zhing sked pa 'phyes// brla kun nag po bcos par bya//
15a2(di): 'bras bu skrang zhing rkang pa na// shin tu sked pa na gyur na// ral gcig rgya mtsho bcos par bya// rtsod na dmug nad srol po la// dar smug po'i thod bcings la grib sel
15a3(di): ma gzugs// gsang ba'i mdos dang bcas la dbul// rkang lag skrang zhing lus mi bde// g.yal zhing sbrid la kha zas lto ru zos pas skyug/ dbyings kyi ma mo'i bka'
15a4(di): chad yin// skom dad che la snying mi dga'// 'gro snying 'dod la gzhan la khro// dam tshig nyams pa'i chad pa yin// rang gi dam tshig gzhung bzhin bskang // 'bras bu
15a5(di): bskang zhing rgyu chu 'gag/ ma mo bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis 'gegs// rnal 'byor ma mo bcu bzhi bcos// klad pa rdol thabs pas khung 'gag/ gnyid mi 'ong zhing gzhan gyis
15a6(di): smras pa gnod// sprul pa ma mo bcos par bya// rgong pa drag pos phral du thebs// lus dang gdong pa skrang nas ni// skra dang kha spun pa na// lha mo g.yu yi bye'u
15a7(di): can bcos// lkog nad 'bras dang phol byung na// lha mo nag mo ched du bcos// gag pa drag po byung gyur na// gtso mo e ka tsa ti bcos// khrag nad rgyu gzer byung
15b1(di): gyur na// nag mo spun gsum bcos par bya// 'brum nag drag po byung gyur na// rgyal mo 'khor bcas nyi shu rtsal ni bcos// bal nad 'dar byung gyur na// sring mo
15b2(di): bzhi ni bcos par byas// srid pa'i sman mo rnams la mchod// skrangs nad 'bems bu byung gyur na// rigs ma 'od ldan bka' skyon yin// rgyas 'debs bzhi la mnyes
15b3(di): par mchod// bas ldag shu ba'i nad byung na// shin tu tsha 'dra ba che gyur na// rma ri rab 'byam bka' skyon yin// ma mo 'dus pa'i gur mdos bya// rus nad gzer
15b4(di): bu byung gyur na// rgyal mo bcu gsum bka' skyon yin// smre sngags drag po'i bskang gso bya// gzer ba drag pos thebs gyur nas// brgyal zhing 'bod pa'i tshul
15b5(di): ston na// skos rje drang dkar gsang mdos bya// skya rengs dang po sha ra tsa na// 'bog cing 'khrigs pa byung gyur na// dkar mo bcu gsum mdos kyis bskang //
15b6(di): de na sa rgyal mo'i gsang bsgrub bsham// gzhung dang mthun pa bsgrub par bya// de nas lcam mo e ka tsa ti dang // lha mo nag mo'i lcags cig mdos// mjug la
15b7(di): rtag nas byas gyur na// nad rnams zhi ba gdon ma za// des kyang zhi bar ma gyur na// nag smug gnyis kyi bsgrub par bya// nga yis nges par bshad pa yin//
16a1(di): shin tu kha smra smros 'gyur ba// gnam sman bcos pa shin tu bshad// gnam sman dkar mo yang dag dpal// bu mo dam tshig g.yu sgron
16a2(di): ma/ gcung mo 'od chags g.yu yi ral gtsog ma// de yi gcung mo parna sha ba ri// de yi gcung mo g.yu'i thong rdeng can// de yi gcung mo nam mkha' khams kyi bo de ma/
16a3(di): de yi gcung mo nam mkha' dpal mo rtsan// gnam sman mched bdun gzhung bzhin bskang // dkar mo nyi khri bdun 'bum gyi// mched bdun kun gyi gtso mo yin// bya thul
16a4(di): can zhes bya ba ni// ji byas ji ru ma btub pas// logs su thugs dam gzhung bzhin bskangs// mched bdun 'khor na ye nas gnas// srog bdag bu mo yin
16a5(di): pas bcos// nad pa sri bu gso ba la// shin tu gdug pas bcos par bya// lha mo nag smug gnyis kyi smyo 'bog ni// shan pas byol song srog pa bzhin// 'phra
16a6(di): zhing kha chu 'ong bar 'gyur// de yi bcos thabs bstan pa ni// nag smug gnyis kyi mdos dang ni// pho mdos mo mdos spel la rgyas par bya// bsgrub pa ma mo'i
16a7(di): gzhung bzhin bya// de nas nag smug sbyin sreg bya// de yis nad rnams zhi bar 'gyur// de yang gdug pa klu yi nad rnams ni// glang thabs spos ri byung gyur na// rigs
16b1(di): ngan gdol pa'i nad rnams yin// dri dang sna tshogs nad rnams 'byung // sa bdag klu yi nad rnams kyang // zha grum 'phye'o bzhin log na// spyi ru bcos pa yo bcos
16b2(di): yin// de ltar nga yis bcos par bya// zhes gsungs so// ma mo srid pa'i bems las/ gdon gyi nad rigs ngos gzung ba'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// /
16b3(di): / de nas yang lha g.yung drung gis 'di skad ces gsol to// kye ma ho 'jig rten 'joms pa'i lha// ma mo gur mdos chen po la// bskang ba'i rdzas rnams ji ltar
16b4(di): lags// zhes gsol te de nyid na 'khod do// nyon cig nga yis bstan par bya// bskyed pa'i khro mo bcu gsum kun kyang gcig/ rdzas kyang gtso mo mi dgos kun kyang gcig
16b5(di): b+h+yo zlog bzhin du bsag par bya// rnal 'byor ma mo bcu bzhi la// nam mkha' snga ma bzhin du bya// mda' ris lnga yang bya ba ste// dkar mo gzi ris mkhar thabs bri//
16b6(di): nyi zla gong nas 'char bar bya// nyi ma'i thod 'phreng can la dbul// stag so chu mig sgril ma yin// mkhar thabs nyi zla stong la gur// shin tu mdzes pa bri bar bya//
16b7(di): 'phra men rgya mtsho'i phyag tu dbul// dbang chen bzhi la za 'og ris// mkhar thabs nyi zla gong nas 'char// de bzhin dbang chen bzhi la bskur// dgyes sde bzhi yi
17a1(di): mda' ris ni// sngon mo bzhi la nya mig ris// shin tu mdzes pa bri bar bya// mkhar thabs nyi zla rtse la 'char// dgyes sde bzhi la
17a2(di): dbul bar bya// phung byed bzhi la chu mig ris// gdan ni phyogs dang bstun pa yin// mkhar thabs nyi zla 'char bar bya// 'khor na gnas pa'i ma mo stong rtsa
17a3(di): brgyad// grangs kyis gnas pa la bsdus te// bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis la/ gong ma bzhin du mchod par bya// gtor ma bzhi yang phyogs bzhir bzhag/ shing ris bsdus
17a4(di): pa snga ma bzhin// rgyang bu dar gyis mtshon pa gsum// gtso bo nyid la dbul bar bya// lnga bcu rtsa bzhi ba la tshon la// tshom bu gsum pa bya bar bshad// ring
17a5(di): thung kun kyang lus kyi tshad// de yang rnal 'byor ma mo 'khor bcas glud// stag gzig la sogs bcu bzhi yang // srog chags tshan pa bcu bzhi tshad// 'bru bya 'bru/
17a6(di): lug grub tshad rnams// lnga bcu rtsa brgyad glung du dbul// de yang sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan// de nas srid pa'i sman mo la// 'bru las byas pa'i sems can sna
17a7(di): tshogs dang // rgyang bu lnga bcu rtsa dgu dang // nam mkha' lnga bcu rtsa dgu dang // ma mo bdun gyi nam mkha' ni// khong pa gnag la kha chag ser// rma bya sgo yis
17b1(di): zer gyis brgyan// sring mo bzhi yi nam mkha' ni// phyogs dang bskrun pa'i khong pa la// kha chag mdzes mtshon btang bar bya// mda' ni zangs yag lcam
17b2(di): mkhris btang // phyogs dang bstun pa so so'i mda'// sring mo bzhi la dbul bar bya// e ka tsa ti spun drug la// gzhung dang mthun pa dbul bar bya//
17b3(di): gsang ba'i yum bzhi'i nam mkha' dang // sna tshogs rdzas rnams bsags pa kun kyang 'thun// de nas ri rab bca' ba ni// sna tshogs 'bru sna'i gsang phye la//
17b4(di): ri rab bang rim bzhi pa bya// rgyung bu khru re 'phang kyang de bzhin no// ri rab thog tu nas dang 'bru yi bang ba bya// de nas la rdzas sna tshogs bang ba bya// sha mar gsu rab
17b5(di): sna tshogs bsham// ri rab steng du bzhag par bya// gser dngul zangs lcags rin chen dbyig/ ri rab steng du bzhag par bya// de nas mngar sna tshang bar bzhag/
17b6(di): de yi steng du za 'og gur chen dbub par bya// rwa bzhi dbus su rma bya lnga// gzhung dang 'thun par gzugs par bya// de nas bang rim dang po la// mthing nag gur
17b7(di): chen dbub par bya// de nas bang rim gnyis pa la// ldang sngon gur chen dbub par bya// de nas bang rim gsum pa la// le brgan gur chen dbub par bya//
18a1(di): de nas bang rim bzhi pa la// sna tshogs dar gyis 'ja' ris bya// dar dang ras sam pags bu bsnams// khri rkang bzhi la rim par
18a2(di): bskor// de nas gzhung bzhin bskang bar bya// ma mo srid pa'i bems chen po las/ gur mdos chen po bskang ba'i rdzas bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// /
18a3(di): / de nas yang g.yung drung lha yis 'di skad ces gsol to// kye ma'o yab cig 'jig rten 'joms mdzad lha// sarba ru ba zhes bya ba thams cad
18a4(di): slong srog ca po 'das// 'di mi bzhang rdzas 'i wAr lags/ nas nas mi nyi nyid na 'khod// de nas yang shin cig 'jig can nas kyig lung druH/
18a5(di): dbyings kyi yum drug rdzas rnams 'thun// rgyal mo drug kyang de bzhin no// ye shes rje mo bcu bzhi mthun// 'khor rnams 'di ru ma gsungs pa// srid pa'i rgyal mo'i
18a6(di): nal mang byung // rgyang bu shing ris kun dang 'thun// srid pa'i sman mo rnams la ni// shing bu ma gsungs rgyang bu byung // bskyed pa'i khru mo rnams la ni// rgyang
18a7(di): bu nam mkha' shing ris rnams// der gyi sna tshogs brgyan par bya// nam mkha' la ni rma bya'i sgo yis brgyan// rnal 'byor ma mo bcu bzhi yi// btsun mo gnyis la
18b1(di): dAr gyis brgyan par bya// khyung ni sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan pa yis// srid pa'i spyan mo'i tshogs la ni// nam mkha' bsags pa kun kyang 'thun// snang ning
18b2(di): srid pa'i sems can gzugs// sna tshogs ngan sgros brgyan par bya// gtsor ni mi gzugs pho mo spe la ma yis// phyogs bzhi ra bdun bdun bzhag par bya//
18b3(di): po ches mo chas mdzes par brgyan// khrag sna mang po'i brgyan pas phor bu brgyan// phyogs bzhi mtshams bzhir bzhag par bya// rin chen snod mchog bum pa bani//
18b4(di): bdud rtsi dza gad sman gyis dgang // tshe yi 'brang rgyas bzhi yis kha bcad de// gtsang ma'i snyan pa ting phyogs bzhir gzhag/ gtsang ma'i mda' ba ni phyogs
18b5(di): bzhir banag/ btsun mo chas bzang bzhi yis phyag gis 'degs pa'i tshul// de nas dang por sna tshogs dar gyi 'phreng bas bskor// de nas ras ma
18b6(di): dkar po'i 'phreng bas bskos// dmar po ser ba sngon po dang // pags bu'i 'phreng bas rgyun zhing bskar// dpyid dang dbyar chas dgun chas dbya// skad snyan
18b7(di): bya dang nor bzang lug/ gser ga yu khrab dang bangs dang lcags// dar dang ba 'og gos dang rgyan// sna tshogs tshang bar bsogs nas ni// gtsong ma'i gnas su
19a1(di): dkar nag sgra phub ste// zhag gsum bsnyen pa phul nas ni// slob dpon gsum gyis so so'i las// ting 'dzin gsar te gzhung
19a2(di): bzhin bya// slob dpon chas gos ldan nas ni// mdos la dang por spyan drangs shing // bar du byung khungs gdon par bya// tha mar dngos kyang gdab par bya//
19a3(di): de nas bskang gso drag tu bya// de nas chad lhag nor ba bshags// de nas gtso mo yum la gyer// de nas yum drug rtag pa'i rgyal mo la// rims kyis tha le
19a4(di): gcad par bya// dbyings kyi yum drug dang rtag pa'i rgyal mo drug/ rje mo bcu bzhi sman mo'i tshogs// kun kyang mdos chen gsum la gcig/ dbyings kyi ma mo'i 'khor
19a5(di): bcas dang rgyal mo drug gi 'khor// sman mo'i 'khor dang bcas pa rnams// b+h+yo zlog mdos las gzhan na med// skos bdag brgyud dang tshe yi lha mo bcu drug ni//
19a6(di): bar snang sa dang bco brgyad pa'o// gzhung gi gzhan las grags pa med// zor bdag bzhi ni kun la gces// tshe yi lha mo bzhi yang dgos// ded dpon bzhi po gzhan
19a7(di): na med// ces gsungs so// ma mo srid pa'i bems chen po las/ skos kyi g.yung drung lnga bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas yang lha g.yung
19b1(di): drung gis 'di skad ces gsungs so// kye ma ho/ rgyal mo'i 'jig rten 'joms mdzad lha// srid pa'i lto ni kun la shis// de nas rgyal mo bcu gsum mdos// de yi
19b2(di): rdzas rnams ji ltar bsags// zhes gsol te de nyid na 'khod do// de nas yang bka' stsal pa/ rgyal mo bcu gsum skong rdzas ni/ mda' chen bya rgod ma bcu gsum la//
19b3(di): me long bcu gsum gyis brgyan pa dang / nam mkha' bcu gsum la/ rma bya'i mdongs bcu gsum gyi sa brgyan pa'o// nam mkha' sngon po gser gyi kha cag can bcu gsum/
19b4(di): nag mo dung gi kha cag can gsum/ ser mo g.yu'i kha cag can gsum/ dmar mo la nag mo'i kha cag can gsum/ khong nag mo la tshon tshogs kyi nam mkha' cig/ 'phang
19b5(di): bcu gsum la me long so sor mdzes tshon btang / de'i tshe rgyan ni sna tshogs dar snas brgyan pa'o// ngar blud bcu gsum ni der chas su bcug la/ kha dog ni nam mkha'
19b6(di): dang mthun pa la gser g.yu'i brgyan pa'o// cig ni che ba la dar mthing nag gi gu zu gser gyi rdo rje kha chag byas pa la nyi zla'i phur sgrogs byas pa bskon pa la/ mthing gi go cho ga
19b7(di): la gser g.yu'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa mgo la bskon pa ni srid pa'i rgyal mo la dbul lo// snying khar me long mtheb gang ba yong gdags so// de yang rgyal mo zhes bya
20a1(di): ba ni dper na sa bdag rgyal pos 'bangs mnga' 'og bsdus nas bka' bsgo ba nyan pa bzhin/ srid pa cham la 'bebs pa'i gtso mo srid pa'i rgyal
20a2(di): mo dbyings kyi yum drug cha ma la phab nas 'khol te/ de'i nang nas chags byed rgyal mo dang / rin chen 'bar ma 'od kyi rgyal mo dang / dga' ma ting 'dzin nyul byed kyi
20a3(di): rgyal mo dang gsum gyis rtag pa'i rgyal mo 'khol srid pa'i bde 'gror rtag pa'i rgyal mo dang / mkha' 'gro'i rgyal mor nam mkha'i dbyings phyug ma dang / mkha' 'gro bkrag
20a4(di): gsal 'od 'bar rgyal mo dang / des tshoms rnal 'byor ma mo bcu bzhi 'khol/ 'dod pa'i rgyal mo 'phra men thugs kyi gzer can ma dang / 'dod pa'i rgyal mo thugs kyi gtso mo
20a5(di): khram thog ma dang / 'dod pa'i rgyal mo rdo rje mkha' 'gro mas ni srid pa'i sman mo rnams 'khol/ de'i nang nas 'dod pa'i rgyal mo nag mo kha rlan mche ba can dang / 'dod pa'i rgyal
20a6(di): mo bdud 'dul ral gcig ma dang / 'dod pa'i rgyal mo dkar mo g.yag thod ma dang / de ltar rgyal mo bcu gsum po des ni ma mo rigs kyi stong rtsa brgyad 'khol lo// srid pa'i
20a7(di): rgyal mos mi 'khol ba ni med do// de nas sngags pa dam tshig nyams nas/ snying mun rum du sros nas nyams lci ba la/ lus ber ba langs nas dran pa mi gsal na bya//
20b1(di): khrag gi phur bu bcu gsum ni thams cad 'dus pa'i zor kha bzlog pa'o// tha mar mdos byang shar mtshams su chu la bskyal lo// gtang ba ni srid pa'i rgyal mo nyid la btang
20b2(di): ngo// khrag gi phur bu ru khrag sna yod tshad las shes rab ma'i mtshal med du mi rungs pas/ bskang la bal tshon sna lnga yis kha bcad la dbul lo// sha chen gyi gtor mcha
20b3(di): gcig dang / dpal gyi gtor ma dang / phud dang / zhal zas kyi tshogs dang / rnga gling dang / swa ra ma ti dang / mar me dang / mchod rdzas dbul bar bya'o//
20b4(di): de nas rnga chen brdung zhing 'di skad gsungs so// kye 'dod khams rgyal mo tshur gson cig/ khyod kyi ming dang mtshan gsol ba// rdo rje gar gyi dbang phyug ma/
20b5(di): pad+ma gar gyi legs ldan gnyis// dpyid zla ra ba'i nya shed la// gnyis med sbyor ba byed pa las// zla dgu dang ni ngo bcu la// bu tsha ming sring dgu zhig btsas// srung
20b6(di): mo chen mo mthu che rtsal drag nas// sa yi rim pa dgu yi 'og tu sras// ming po skos kyi bdag po brgyad// gling bzhi yi ni bdag por bskos// mi srid de ni dgu ru srid/
20b7(di): sa dgu'i gting du sbas pa de// ro langs su cig 'gul 'gul byung // 'dzam bu'i gling yang gul 'gul 'gul// da ni sku gcig kyang 'gul 'gul ni ma mdzad cig/
21a1(di): 'dzam bu'i gling yang ni 'gul zhing ldeg/ sa g.yos 'ongs par nus pa'o// zhabs gcig 'gul 'gul ni ma mdzad cig/ zhabs gcig
21a2(di): 'gul 'gul ni mdzad pa na// sa bdag klu yang brgyal bar nus// zhabs gnyis thur du brkyang tsam na// gcig ni klu yi yul du brkyang // gcig ni sa bdag mgo dgu
21a3(di): 'dul// klu yi yul du brkyang ba yis// bde byed klu rgyal gyi thugs kyang dkrugs// 'byung ba klu yi tsha ba snyoms// dbu gcig bteg bteg ma mdzad cig/ dbu ni bar
21a4(di): snang khams su 'phye// lha zan kun kyang 'dar zhing brgyal// spyan gnyis dmar ba'i rtsa bzlog pas// bar snang lha bran kun kyang 'khol// srid gsum la ni mnga' mdzad
21a5(di): ma/ lo gsar gnyan pa'i tshes gcig la// rgyal mo ni sku bzhongs la// mdos kyi ni phud la spyon// s+pha ra ma ti'i mchod pa bzhes// sha chen gtor ma ni 'di bzhes
21a6(di): shig/ mdzes pa'i sgra snyan ni 'di la spyon// 'od ldan gsal ba ni me long dang // mda' bzang ni bya rgod ma// dpal dar ni ru mtshon dang // za 'og ni lding khang na//
21a7(di): gsal ba yi mar me bltam// ma dud spos mchog ni na bun du 'thul// sems rlung nam mkha' bkra gsal 'bar// khrag sna'i rba rlabs ni ci li li// mo 'phang mdo long ya
21b1(di): si li li// chas su btsal nas rgyal mo spyan 'dren no// dza huM baM ho/ ra tsa ma snying kha rak+ta ti badz+ra b+h+yo/ ru lu ru lu hUM b+h+yo hUM/ zhes spyan drangs la dkyil 'khor gyi dbus su
21b2(di): dpal chen po'i mdun du bzhugs te/ mdos la byin gyis brlabs par bsam mo// de nas rim gyis spyan drang ba ni 'di skad ces brjod do// kye 'dod pa'i
21b3(di): ma mo tshur gson cig/ chags byed rgyal mo rin 'od 'bar rgyal mo dang // ting 'dzin nyul mdzad rgyal tsho'i tshogs// sngon gyi bskal pa dang po la// sangs rgyas ma byung snga/
21b4(di): rol na// mnga' mdzad rgyal mo bcu gsum byung // chags byed ma dang rin chen 'od 'bar ma// dga' ma ting 'dzin nyul byed ma// srid pa'i bde 'gror nam mkha'i dbyings
21b5(di): phyug ma// bkra gsal 'od zer 'bar ba gsum// 'phra men thugs kyi zer can dang // bdud kyi gtso mo khram thogs rgyal mo dang // 'dod pa'i rgyal mo khram thogs rdo rje
21b6(di): khros ma dang // gtso mo la sogs bcu gsum mo// 'dzam bu gling la dbang sgyur ma// 'jig rten mthu dang dpal mdzad ma// do nub mdos la spyan 'dren no//
21b7(di): mnga' bdag rgyal mo gshegs su gsol// ri rab khri 'phang dang po las// chags byed rgyal mo rin chen 'bar ba'i 'od kyi rgyal mo dang // dga' bas ting 'dzin drod yul
22a1(di): rgyal mo gsum// 'od chen 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor nas// kun kyang mi bzad 'bar ba'i sku// gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor du// sna
22a2(di): tshogs rdzas rnams bsogs nas ni// dbyings kyi rgyal mo spyan 'dren na// mdo sa la byin gyis rlob cing spyon// bskang ba'i rdzas chen mchod pa 'di// gtsang zhing dag
22a3(di): par sbyar ba la// bdud rtsi mchog dang nor gyi dbyig/ gos dang rgyan dang mdzes pa'i nor// snyan pa'i sgra mchog 'di 'bul gyis// rnal 'byor mthu dang dpal bskyed la//
22a4(di): mi mthun rkyen chen slar la bzlog/ srid pa'i bde 'gror rtag pa'i rgyal mo dang // nam mkha'i rgyal mo mkha' 'gro dbyings phyug ma// mkha' 'gro bkra gsal rgyal mo gsum//
22a5(di): bang rim gnyis la sku bzhugs te// 'od chags mthing ka'i dkyil 'khor nas// gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor 'dir// 'thun pa'i rdzas tshan ba sogs pa la//
22a6(di): spyan 'dren mchod kyis gshegs su gsol// kun kyang mthing nag 'bar ba'i sku// mdos la byin gyi rlob cing spyon// bskang ba'i rdzas chen mchod pa 'di// gtsang
22a7(di): zhing dag par bshams pa la// bdud rtsi mchog dang nor gyi dbyig/ gos dang rgyan dang mdzes pa'i nor// snyan pa'i sgra mchog 'di 'bul gyis// rnal 'byor mthu dang
22b1(di): dpal skyed cig/ mi mthun rkyen chen slar la bzlog/ mnga' thang rkyen du bzhes su gsol// kye 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ thugs kyi gzer
22b2(di): chen 'dod pa'i rgyal mo dang // bdud mo kun gyi gtso mo khram thogs rgyal mo dang // rdo rje khros ma 'dod pa'i rgyal mo rnams// ma mo kun gyi rgyal mos bya// ri rab bang
22b3(di): rim gsum pa la bzhugs pa// kun kyang khro mo ldang nag sku// gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor du// sna tshogs 'thun pa'i rdzas bsogs nas// rnal 'byor
22b4(di): rgyal mo spyan 'dren na// mdos la byin gyis brlab cing sbyin// bskang 'i sa chen mchod pa 'di// gtsang zhing dag par sbyar ba la// bdud rtsi mchog dang nor
22b5(di): gyi dbyig/ gos dang rgyan dang mdzes pa'i nor// snyan pa'i sgra mchog 'di 'bul gyis// rnal 'byor mthu dang dpal bskyed la// mi mthun rkyen chen slar la bzlog
22b6(di): kye 'dod pa'i mamo tshur gson cig/ nag mo kha rlon mche ba can// 'dod pa'i ma mo bdud 'dul ral gcig ma// 'dod pa'i ma mo dkar mo g.yag
22b7(di): thod can// ri rab bang rim tha ma las// khrag mtsho dmar po'i dkyil 'khor nas// kun kyang dmar nag 'bar ba'i sku// gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor du//
23a1(di): sna tshogs mthun pa'i rdzas sogs te// sman mo rgyal mo spyan 'dren na// mdos la byin gyis rlob cing spyon// bskang ba'i rdzas chen mchod pa
23a2(di): 'di/ gtsang zhing dag par bshams pa la// bdud rtsi mchog dang nor gyi dbyig/ gos dang rgyan dang mdzes pa'i nor// snyan pa'i sgra mchog 'di 'bul gyis//
23a3(di): rnal 'byor tshe dang dpal bskyed la// mi mthun gdug pa'i rkyen chen bzlog/ mnga' bdag rgyal mo bcu gsum yang // gsang ba'i dam rdzas 'di na 'thun par ba sogs//
23a4(di): bzang dgu bsde bas nas sku glud 'bul// rgyal mo bcu gsum thugs dam bskang // ma mo bye ba 'bum phrag 'khor du skyong // 'dir gshegs mchod pa dam par
23a5(di): bzhes// zhes spyan drangs la/ de nas khungs byung / de nas 'di skad ces brjod do// sngon gyi bskal pa dang po la// mdos byung de ni ji ltar byung // glud byung de
23a6(di): ni gang na byung // rgya gar gyi yul shed du// mi nad ni chu ltar 'khrug/ phyug nad ni rlung ltar 'tshub// ci bgyis pa ci ma sman// paN+Di mched gsum gyis ni smon lam btab//
23a7(di): ser sna'i phra skor nas// gsang ba'i 'bum sde'i nang shed nas// srid pa'i mdos le'u chen po btus// pho dang mo'i mdos la// nyin gsum ni sogs su bring //
23b1(di): mtshan gsum ni gyer bu bskyer// cha gcig ni ri rab rtse ru bskyal// cha gcig ni lung gsum mdo ru bskyal// cha gcig ni chab kyi gzhung la bskyal// de nas mdos
23b2(di): byung ni gang nas byung // glud byung ni gang nas byung // bal po'i yul du byung // bal po ni hUM mdzad kyis// bal po rgyal po'i don du mdzad// rgyal mo bcu gsum
23b3(di): gyi glung du 'bul// brgyal ba'i snying nad kyang der sang ngo // de nas mdos byung gang nas byung // zhang zhung yul shed du// zhang zhung gi rgyal po la// mkhris pa ni gsha'
23b4(di): yas zin// ji bgyis ni ji ma sman// mu dun shag kyi pra phab pas// ho ra ta lcam mo ni bcu gsum la// grungad dang thabs cig 'bul// rgyal po'i bsun las
23b5(di): der sos so// zhang zhung pon po khri mun stang gis// ka dgu ni bsog ga sog nas// 'thun dgu ni sdeb nas su// rgyal mo bcu gsum la glud du phul// bsnyun nad
23b6(di): kyang der ba sangs so// de nas mdos byung gang nas byung // glud byung ni gang nas byung // bod yul gyi dbus su byung // spu rgyal btsan po ni bsnyun gyis zin// ji baM gyis
23b7(di): ni ji ma sman// rgya gar gyi yul grong khyer gsal ldan nas// dza ya se ni spyan drangs nas// pra phab ni cha bskor nas// ma bdud rgyal mo ni skyon no skad// rgya bod
24a1(di): mkhas pa ni mang pos bskor// nyin gsum ni sogs su bsogs// mtshan gsum ni gyer du bskyer// cha gcig ni ri gsum rtse la bskyal//
24a2(di): cha gcig lung gsum gyi mdo ru bskyal// cha gcig rtsang chab kyi gzhung la bskyal lo// rgyal po snyun las der thar ro// do nub tsam su'i glud// yon bdag rgyu sbyor glud/
24a3(di): rdo rje'i slob dpon gyud// mched dang ni lum drul grud// rgyal mo bcu gsum la glung du 'bul// mdos bdag ni mdos bzhes shig/ glung bdag ni glud 'phrul lo// de na/
24a4(di): byung sa gdab pa ni// ma mchis ni dgye dgu zhig mchis// dgal dgu ni bsogs nas mchis// mthun dgu ni sdebs nas mchis// cho ma ni chos dgu mchis// mda' bya//
24a5(di): rgod ma bcu gnyis na// phod sgro lde ma ru dang bcu gsum mchis// dar sna bcu gnyis na// dpal dar yug chen dang bcu gsum mchis// nam mkha' bcu gnyis
24a6(di): na/ mdza' ris 'od sngon dang bcu gsum mchis// rgyang bu ni bcu gnyis na// khug rang 'byung dang bcu gsum mchis// rma byin bcu gnyis na// 'dab ldan ser po
24a7(di): dang bcu gsum mchis// mo 'phang ldem mo ni bcu gnyis na// gser ris ni 'khor lo dang bcu gsum mchis// mdzes pa'i mtshon bcu gnyis na// gzi ldan 'od chags dang //
24b1(di): bcu gsum mchis// khrag sna'i phor pa ni bcu gnyis na// mtshal khrag zag dgu dang bcu gsum mchis// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnyen po ni// rgyal mo bcu gsum
24b2(di): gyi spyan snga na// 'dza' gang bdud rtsi'i bcud bltam nas// rag+na rgya mtsho rba rlabs ni ci li li// gsal ba'i mar me ni 'od bltam nas// bdug spos chen po ni thu lu lu//
24b3(di): mthing nag gur chen ni lji ri ri// sha chen gtor ma ni tsi li li// chu lug rgya mo ni 'ba' dang di ri ri// 'bras bu me tog sna tshogs ni btsal du bkram// zhal zas sna
24b4(di): tshogs mchod pa ri ltar spungs// ma mo mkha' 'gro dang re spro// rdza rnga sil snyan skad re snyan// mtshogs mkha' 'gro dam la 'du// do nub ni mdos kyir ro// lba
24b5(di): yang ni gyer ma bsnol// mi yang ni ma gzims shig/ nam mkha' ni kyid bkyil// rgod po ni khyung lding yang // 'greng mi'i ni glud ma lags// dud phyugs kyi ni
24b6(di): sbyin ma lags// bdud phyugs kyi ni rgyal mor bya// ri logs ni ya gi na// sha sgro na smig rgyu yang // 'greng mi'i glung ma lags// dud phyugs kyi ni sbyin ma
24b7(di): lags// ma bdud kyi ni rgyal mo'i bskor// mtsho mo ni ma ki la// gyur sram ma bu ni skye gzhung yang // 'greng mi'i glud ma lags// du da phyugs kyi yang sbyin ma
25a1(di): lags// ma bdu da rgyal mo bskod// do nub 'greng mi'i ni glung du 'bul// dud phyugs kyi yang sbyin cig gsob// kye
25a2(di): 'dod pa'i rgyal mo tshur gson cig/ chags byed rgyal mo tshur gson cig/ sku ni mthing nag 'bar ba la// mthing gi go cho ga dbu la gsol// mthing nag ral pa 'od du 'bar//
25a3(di): sku la dar nag go zu gsol// mi mgo rlon pa'i 'phreng bas brgyan// dar nag ru mtshon g.yas na bsnams// g.yan na 'phrul gyi me long bsnams// sngobasangs ni bka'
25a4(di): blo na mdzad// khro gnyer can ni gung blon mdzad// nang blon mo ni spyi rings ma// rgyal mo khyod kyi 'khor bcas la// gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor 'di 'bul gyis//
25a5(di): rgyal mo'i bka 'chad da bzlog la// gsang ba mdos 'di pha ra la song // rgyang bu 'phan rings sku yi glud// rgyal mo sku lus 'od ldan pas// dam tshig nyams pa'i bka'
25a6(di): chad zhi// rma bya mdongs chen 'di phul bas// bkrag dang gzi byin ldan par dbu la// sems kyi glud du nam mkha' 'bul// tshe yi glud du mo 'phang ljang mo dbul//
25a7(di): srog gi glud du mda' bzang bya rgod dbul// gos kyi glud du dar nag gle chen 'bul// rnam shes glud du khro lcags mde'u rtse dbul// rgyal mo rnams ni ma rig 'khrul pas
25b1(di): bcings// ma rig bag chags sel mdzad pas// snang srid gsal ba'i le long dbul// rgyal mo rnams kyi bka' chad bzlog pa'i phyir// sna tshogs khrag sna mtshal
25b2(di): chen zag dgu dbul// rgyal mo'i thugs nad sangs gyur la// bdag cag g.yar dam so ru stsol// ma dud spos chen 'brang rgyas dang // 'dza' gang bdud rtsi 'di
25b3(di): 'bul lo// rgyal mo khyed kyi thugs dam skongs gyur cig/ bdag cag g.yar dam so ru stsol// pe ta gling gi rgyal mo khyod// mdos bdag lags kyi mdos long la//
25b4(di): glungad bdag lags kyi glud bzhes shig/ mnga' ba dag rkyen du bzhes nas kyang // tshe srings dpal bskyed dngos grub gsol// mdos bdag chen po glud pa zhes shig/
25b5(di): ces mchod do// de nas 'dza' ga da gtams la 'di skad do// kye 'dod pa'i rgyal mo tshur gson cig/ rin chen 'od 'bar rgyal mo ni// sku ni ldang
25b6(di): nag 'bar ba la// thugs ni ma g.yos dkyil mo che// g.yas pa thod pa khrag gis bkang ba bsnams// g.yon na sdig pa'i g.yang gzhi 'phyar// srid pa gsum
25b7(di): la mnga' mdzad ma// 'dod khams rgyal mo chen mo khyod// khams gsum zhal du rabs gdeng nas// stong gsum zhal du rab tu gsol// bzod par dka' ba
26a1(di): dur khrod chen mo na// mi khrag rta khrag mtsho ru bskyil// 'gro ba'i mdangs la mnga' mdzad ma// khyod kyi sngon dmar gsang sngags la//
26a2(di): sna tshogs mi nad phyugs nad gtong // mdos bdag ni mdos pazhes la// glud bdag ni glud bzhes shig/ ces phud btang ngo // de nas ting nge 'dzin
26a3(di): gyi rgyal mo la 'di skad do// kye 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ dga' ma ting 'dzin drod yul rgyal mo ni// sku mdog sngo sangs khro mo'i sku// dbu la mu tig
26a4(di): ljon tshar gsol// sku la ljang nag gu zu la// mu tig 'phreng bas kha chags gsal// phyag g.yas zhing chen rgyam mtshan bsnams// g.yon na 'khor lo mtshon cha
26a5(di): bsnams// 'dul ba'i kha chen drug po 'dul// 'khor ni ma mo brgya bcus bskor// gsol ni sha khrag dmar chen gsol// rdzas su cang kha'u ri sel// nor
26a6(di): bu 'bar ba'i kha da thang bzangs sel// grogs su gnod sbyin stobs ldan nag po brten// 'bar ba mar mo'i 'od dang bcas// mdos bdag ni mdos longs shig/
26a7(di): glung bdag ni glud pa zhes shig/ ces phud btang ngo // kye 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ srid pa'i bde 'gro rtag pa'i rgyal mo ni// sku ni cir
26b1(di): yang ma nges te// sku la mthing gi go cho ga gsol// rma lo mdzes pa'i lan tshar can// phyag na ba dan 'khor lo bsnams// 'khol ni rnal 'byor ma mo 'khol//
26b2(di): mdos bdag ni mdos lang la// glung bdag ni glud bzhes shig/ 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ mkha' 'gro rgyal mo nam mkha'i dbyings phyug ma// sna tshogs
26b3(di): 'gyur ba'i gzugs 'chang zhing // 'khor lo ral gri phyag na bsnams// mthing nag mdzes pa'i go zu la// ut+pal sngon pos kha chags can// dbu skra mthing
26b4(di): nag thor tshugs can// kha blon gung blon nang blon tshogs dang bcas// 'byung ba nam mkha'i mnga' bdag mo// 'dul ni rnal 'byor ma mo 'dul// mdos bdag chen
26b5(di): mo mdos long la// glud bdag ni glud bzhes shig/ kye 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson dang // mkha' 'gro'i rgyal mo bkra gsal 'od// sku ni ser nag 'bar ba la//
26b6(di): ser nag ral pa'i thor tshugs can// lag na rin chen ban d+ha bsnams// zhal gdangs mche ba gtsigs pa ni// nyid kyi 'khor rnams ma lus 'dul// khro gnyer bzhad
26b7(di): pas rnal 'byor ma mo 'dul// mdos bdag chen mo mdos pazhes shig/ glung bdag chen mo glud bzhes shig/ ces phud btang ngo // kye 'dod pa'i
27a1(di): ma mo tshur gson cig/ 'phra men thugs kyi gzer can rgyal mo ni// sku ni smyug mthing chen mo la// dbu skra dma' lo mdzes pas brgyan//
27a2(di): me dpung dmar po'i dkyil na bzhugs// sku la 'phra men go zu gsol// gza' chen brgyad kyi kha chags can// nyi zla shar ba'i go mtshon can// phyag g.yas rin
27a3(di): chen ga'u mdzes pa'i chun 'phyang ba snams// ma mo bdun la mnga' mdzad ma// 'dul ni srid pa'i tshogs rnams 'dul// mdos bdag chen mo mdos pa zhes la//
27a4(di): glud bdag chen mo glud pa zhes shig/ kye/ 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ khram thogs bdud mo gtso mo'i rgyal mo ni// khram kha stong la dbang sgyur
27a5(di): ba/ dmag gi rgyal mo bzhi la mnga' mdzad ma// 'dul ni srid pa'i mtshogs 'dul// sku ni mthing nag 'bar ba la// na bza' dar nag go zu gsol// g.yas
27a6(di): pa kha T+wAM rtse gsum bsnams// g.yon na spyang mo mgo dgu bsnams// zhal du mi snying 'bum 'bum gsol// bdud kyi dmag dpung 'joms mdzad ma// mdos
27a7(di): bdag legs kyis mdes pazhes shig/ glung bdag ni glud bzhes shig/ 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ rgyal mo chen mo kha rlan mche ba can// sman mo lnga bcu rtsa drug la//
27b1(di): mnga' bdag rgyal mo mnga' mdzad ma// srid pa'i byol kha bzlog mdzad ma// sku mdog nag mo tse re re// thod pa khrag gis bkang ba g.yas na bsnams// g.yon na
27b2(di): mi snying phrul lu lu// sdang ba'i las ngan dgra bo la// las kyi thun cig dbab tu gsol// 'khor 'dul rgyal mo khong dig shags// ma mo bdun gyi rgyal ma khyod//
27b3(di): mdos bdag ni mdos longs la// glud bdag ni glung pa zhes shig/ 'dod pa'i me mo tshur gson cig/ bdud 'dul rgyal mo ral gcig ma// sku mdog byi ru dam
27b4(di): mo la/ mu men zangs kyi gozugasal// phyag g.yas 'od ma'i rgyud bskul zhing // g.yon pa zhags pa dmar po stsogs// nyams pa rnams kyi snying khrag 'thung //
27b5(di): mdos bdag ni mdos long la// glung bdag ni glud bzhes shig/ 'dod pa'i ma mo tshur gson cig/ 'dod pa'i rgyal mo dkar mo g.yag thod mo// sku mdog shel dkar
27b6(di): ldem pa la// rma lo g.yu yi thig le can// dbu la dung gi go cho ga gsol// sku la dar dkar gzu gsol// mi mgo thod pa'i 'phreng bas brgyan// sring mo
27b7(di): bzhi la dbang sgyur zhing // gsang ba'i ma mo bzhi la mnga' mdzad ma// srid pa'i gru 'degs bzhi ni khyod kyis 'khol// mdos bdag chen mo mdos longs la//
28a1(di): glud bdag chen mo glud bzhes shig/ gsang ba mdos kyi dkyil 'khor 'di 'bul gyis// rgyal mo rnams kyi bka' chad 'dis bzlog la/
28a2(di): gsang ba mdos 'di phar la long // rgyang bu 'phan rings sku yi glud// rgyal mo'i sku lus 'od ldan pas// dam tshig nyams pa'i bka' chad zhi// rma bya mdos chen
28a3(di): 'di 'bul bas// bkrag dang gzi mdangs ldan par dbu la// sems kyi glud du nam mkha' 'bu la// tshe yi glud du mo 'phang sngon me 'bul// srog gi glud du mda'
28a4(di): bzang bya rgod dbul// gos kyi glud du dar nag gle'u chen dbul// rnam shes glud du khro lcags mde'u rtse 'bul// rgyal mo rnams kyi ma rig 'khrul pas bcings// ma
28a5(di): rig bag chags sel mdzad pa// snang srid gsal ba'i me long dbul// rgyal mo rnams kyi bka' chad bzlog pa'i phyir// sna tshogs khrag sna ma tshal chen za gu 'bul//
28a6(di): rgyal mo'i thugs nad sangs gyur na// bdag cag dbyar dam gso ru gsol// ma bdud spos chen 'brang rgyas dang // 'dza' gad bdud rtsi 'di dbul lo// rgyal
28a7(di): mo khyed kyi thugs dam skongs gyur cig/ bdag cag dbyar dam gso ru gsol// pe ta gling gi rgyal mo khyod// mdos pa dag lags kyi mdos longs la// glud bdag
28b1(di): lags kyis glud bzhes shig/ mnga' thang rkyen du bzhes nas kyang // tshe bsrings dpal bskyed dngos grub gsol// mdos bdag chen po mdos 'di bzhes// glud
28b2(di): bdag chen po glud longs shig/ glung thams cad ni pho glud mo glud de kun kyang mthun no// de nas rma bya'i mdongs kyis byad sgrib tu bcug la/ pho glung mo glud la
28b3(di): 'di brjod do// kye rin chen spos kyi mi bo che// yon bdag ni pho mo'i glud// rin chen ni sna lnga'i gzugs// lung thang mig la 'gron bu'i so// rus pa dkar
28b4(di): po ni mi la mchis// rus pa'i glud du dung khang byi rus 'bu la// mi la ni sha mchis te// sha'i glud du dbul lo// sha'i bal ni spos skyes mchis// khrag
28b5(di): gi ni glud mchis so// rgya mtshal ni lcug ma la// khrag gi ni glud dbul lo// mi la ni khrag mchis te// snying gi ni glud dbul lo// zho sha ni rtsa bzhi dbul//
28b6(di): ma kha la ma'i glud dbul lo// ba mkhal ni smug po 'bu la// so yi ni glud dbul lo// 'gron bu ni sul mangs dbul// mig
28b7(di): gi ni glud dbul lo// lung thang ni nag po dbul// skra yi glud 'bul lo// gzungs mo ni byi thur dbul// 'gram gyi glud 'bul lo// ba se bo ni lo 'brum dbul//
29a1(di): tshe'i glud 'bul lo// zangs ma ni gnyen gyi tshe// srog gi ni glud dbul lo// ga nam lcags ni dur mo dbul// mi la ni mdangs mchis
29a2(di): teta tarma bya'i mdongs chen dbul// rnam shes tshogs brgyad kyi glud du 'bul// rin po che sna lnga dang / rgya long dang / me long dbul/ lus la dar za ba ni bskon te
29a3(di): dbul// mgo la sa la sil ni brgyan te dbul// g.yas na dar thad ni bu ru ru// g.yon na mi khyer ni lam sel ma// ma bdud rgyal mo'i spyan sngar mchis// bam
29a4(di): mkhal thag sa 'thags tsam rdo re thog/ phye 'thag 'gram skya tsam rdo re thog/ chu chun 'gram gshe ra tsam rdo re thog/ bang chen ri rgyud tsam rdo re thog/ rin chen ni ngar gyi sa
29a5(di): 'di skad zhus// ma bdud rgyal mo ni tshur gson dang // rje dang 'bangs su ni brje bar zhu// tshe dang glud du ni brje bar zhu// ltas ngan sna dgu ni bzlog par zhu//
29a6(di): yas kyi bdud g.yos kyang slar la bzlog/ mas kyi sri langs ni slar la bzlog/ de skad ces zhus pa dang / mu bdud rgyal mo'i zhal na re// smra ba ngag snyan ni ljongs
29a7(di): se ldongs// 'gro na stabs sdug ni lag ma leg/ khyod kyi rje'i glung du ni mchis pa na// smra ba tshig gsum ni nyan mi nyan// 'gro ba gom gsum ni mgyogs mi
29b1(di): mgyogs// gser dang do cig sngo mi sngo// btsan dang kha lta ni phod mi phod// mi dang glud du rje mi rje// mi dang glud du ni de sngo ba na// kha gser dang kha ga yu'i ni yod
29b2(di): dam med// de tsug ni yod pa na// rje dang ni 'bangs su ni rje// de skad ces gsol pa dang // rin chen ngar gyi mched na re// ma bdud rgyal mo tshur gson cig/
29b3(di): gser dang ni de sngo bas// mi lus ni gser bas brin// btsan dang ni kha yang lta// btsan yang mi yis 'khol// mi dang ni glud du mi rjeru// mi bas ni
29b4(di): glud kyang bzang // de skad ces gsol pa dang // mi dang glud du ni do cig bsngo// kha ga ser dang kha ga yu rdog/ rje dang 'bangs su mi rje ru// rje'i glud du 'bangs
29b5(di): re bzang // kye ma bdud rgyal ma bdud rgyal ma ni tshur gson cig/ kye mdos 'di ma bdud rgyal mo'i phyag tu 'bul// dang po yang ma bdud rgyal mi la//
29b6(di): bsha' bsha' ni bsngo bsngo nas// da yang ni ma bdud rgyal mo la 'bul// smra tshig gsum mkhas de ni bsgo ba nyan// 'gro gom gsum mgyogs te bang chen per//
29b7(di): ma bdud rgyal mo'i bka' stsa la nyan// ces ngar gyis smras pas/ rgyal mo thugs dgyes nas glung bzhes pa'o// de nas rgyal mo la mdos btang ba 'di
30a1(di): skad do// kye rgyal mo brgyad cu rtsa lnga'i glud du 'bul// rgyal mo bcu gsum gyi gtso mo ni// ma mo srid pa'i rgyal mos byas//
30a2(di): rgyal mo khyod kyi tshe dang 'brang smos pa// sa gzhi ni sku yi gdan// dog mo ni chu las chags// mtsho ma 'phangs kyi steng shed na// sku mnyag gcig ni ldem
30a3(di): pa'i tshe// da bu ni bar snang khams su 'khol// zhabs ni rgya mtsho'i gting du 'khrug/ phyag ni srin po'i yul du brkyang // zhal ni mi yi yul du gdengs//
30a4(di): sku ni ri rab zo ma la bzhugs// mche ba rol mtsho'i gting du gtsigs// spyan ni stong gsum kun la gzigs// dbu skra sum cu rtsa gsum gnas su bsleb//
30a5(di): rgyal mo khyod kyi lto ba nas// lha dang lha min gyi g.yul ngo 'gyed// rgyal mo khyod kyi lto ba nas// rten 'brel ni bcu gnyis 'char// rgyal mo khyod kyi lto ba nas//
30a6(di): nyon mongs ni dug gsum 'char// yi dgas dmyal ba ni mgo drug kyang // rgyal mo khyod kyi ni sku la 'char// dga' ba'i tshal dang ni 'dres pa'i tshal// ri rab
30a7(di): rtse yi tshal bzhi yang // rgyal mo nyid las kyang byung ba ste// 'byung ba kun gyi ni bcud bdag mo// srid pa cha ma la ni 'bebs mdzad ma// ma mo kha rlang 'od du
30b1(di): 'khrugs// 'jig rten rims nad gtong mdzad ma// rgya mtsho'i gting du zhabs brkyang bas// klu bran 'bum sde dbang du sdud// bar snang khams su 'phyos
30b2(di): pa ni/ lha bran mang po dbang du sdud// srin po'i yul du ni phyag brkyang bas// srin mo rnams ni grogs su byas// mi yi yul du zhal gzigs pas//
30b3(di): sngon dmar mi'i yul du ni khrag nad gtong // ri rab ngos la sku bzhugs pas// thams cad 'byung ba ma mos byas// mche ba ro mtsho'i nang gtsigs pas// srid pa'i
30b4(di): me bdun las la 'khol// stong gsum kun tu spyan gzigs pas// 'gro ba'i srog la mnga' mdzad ma// dbu skra sum cu rtsa gsum gnas su bsleb// lha
30b5(di): rnams ni cha ma la 'beb ma// ma mo ma mo mi rgya'i ru// thams cad 'byung bas ma mos bya// chos kyi dbyings dang dbyer med gcig/ sku ni mthong nag chen mo la//
30b6(di): thugs ni ma g.yos dkyil mo che// sna tshogs 'ja' ltar ldi ri ri// bzhengs shig chos kyi dbyings nas bzhengs// 'jig rten rngam pa'i sgra byung bas// snang srid
30b7(di): thams cad zil gyis gnon// lo gsar gnyen po'i tshe gcig la// rgyal mo ni sku bzhengs shig/ phyag na mi 'phreng mi srang chen mo bsnams// mi brgya khram la thob la
31a1(di): rta brgya srang la 'jal// mdos bdag chen mo mdos long la// glung bdag chen mo glud pa zhes shig/ dbyings kyi rgyal mor gshegs su gsol/
31a2(di): dbyar gyi rgyal mor mdzad pa'i tshe// me tog kun gyi mdangs 'phrog ma// ston gyi rgyal mor mdzad pa'i tshe// me tog snar mo'i bcud 'byin ma// dgun gyi rgyal mo mdzad pa'i
31a3(di): tshebasgrub pa po yi grogs mdzad ma// rgyal mo lnga bcu rtsa lnga'i gtso mo khyod// mdos bdag lags kyis mdos long la// glud bdag lags kyis glung pa zhes
31a4(di): shig/ rgyal mo bcu gsum khyed rnams kyis// mdos 'di phar song slar ma bzlog/ 'di la phya dang ga yang ma 'bros// zhes sring mo bzhini sgo ba ste// shar gyi
31a5(di): dkar mo spyan gsum mche ba can// sring mo rdo rje mdos long la// klud bdag lags kyi glud pa zhes shig/ rgyal mo bcu gsum mche ba can// ming po rnal 'byor mangs
31a6(di): gtong ngo // lho yi nag mo spyan gsum mche ba can// ming po rnal 'byor mdos gtong gis// sring mo rdo rje mdos long nag/ nub kyi dmar po spyan gsum mche ba can//
31a7(di): ming ba rdo rje mdos gtong giso// sring mo rdo rje mdos long zhig/ byang gi sngon mo spyan gsum mche ba can// rnal 'byor mang ba mdos gtong ngo // sring mo rdo rje mangs
31b1(di): long zhig/ sgo ba'i las su sgo phye la// 'phrang ba'i las su 'phrang so la cig/ mdos 'di cha gcig ri ga sum rtse la bskya la// bdag cag rnal 'byor bsgrub pa pos//
31b2(di): ri be bas kyang lhun sdug pa// bkra shis dam pa'i mchog gyur cig/ mdos 'di cha gcig rtsang chab gzhung la bskyal// mi mtha' chu yi rgyun bzhin 'gyur// cha gcig
31b3(di): lung gsum gyi mdo ru bskyal// longs spyod tshogs rnams 'du 'gyur zhes// mdos bdag kyang btang / tshe dgug/ khrag gi por bu zor bdag bzhi la bskul la zor du 'phang
31b4(di): ngo/ ma me srid pa'i bems las/ rgyal mo bcu gsum gyi mdos kyi le'u ste bdun pa'o// // de nas g.yung drung lha yis 'di skad ces gsol to// /
31b5(di): kye ma'i 'jig rten stobs kyi lha// sna tshogs sdig pa'i ltas ngan ji ltar bzlog/ sdig pa'i ltas ngan gang la bgyi// zhes gsol bas/ 'di skad ces bka'
31b6(di): stsal pa/ nyon cig khyod kyi dri ba legs// 'khor ba dus kyi cha 'di la// dus kyi ltas ngan mi la babs// 'ug pa mkhar la tshangs bca' dang // srod la bya skad glog
31b7(di): ba ni/ tam bdud bya sman ltas ngan yin// srin byararo byung zer ba dang // lha bya gong mo khyim du zhugs pa ni// sman dang 'gong po'i ltas ngan yin// bya rgod mkhar la snga
32a1(di): 'dzings pa// ya bdud rgyal po'i ltas ngan yin// yugs sa pho mo sder 'dzings pa// 'brog srin spun bdun ltas ngan yin// rta g.ya/
32a2(di): mtshe ma byung ba ni// byi ba 'gong po'i ltas ngan yin// mgo rku ba log pa'i sems can yang // de yang byi ba 'gong pa'i ltas ngan yin// ming sring bsnol dang bag
32a3(di): shor ba// dam sri nag mo'i ltas ngan yin// glang po che yi mtsho 'dzings pa// brag btsan rgyal po'i ltas ngan yin// sha phe rwa 'dzings bdud kyi ltas ngan yin// mi
32a4(di): dang byo la song bslad pa ni// gnam sman mched bdun ltas ngan yin// sbal pa khyim du tshangs bcas nas// sgeg sgeg sgra skad 'don pa ni// sa bdag gzhi yi ltas
32a5(di): ngan yin// sbrul gyi gshog sgra 'phur ba mthong // byol song klu yi ltas ngan yin// sre mo byi ro sngon du bsgyur// ma btsun rgyal mo'i ltas ngan yin// bya rog 'ug
32a6(di): pas ded nas khyim du babs// li byin har gyi ltas ngan yin// bud med lus mi bde 'gyur la// lus las bu ni mi btsa' bas// sbub dang chu ru byung ba ni// li byi
32a7(di): har gyi ltas ngan yin// de nas bzlog pa ji ltar bgyis// 'jig rten stobs ldan bka' stsol cig/ nyon cig 'jig rten stobs kyi lha// mi dang byol song bslad pa
32b1(di): ni/ ta'abru bya dkar mo ma chu dmar bdun// lug dkar mo bdun/ khyi dkar mo yod na bdun/ med kyang shel mi gcig la// dar sna tshogs kyis brgyan nas/
32b2(di): dar ser pos mgul nas btags la/ de man chad du lug mig dmar gyis sna grangs la bzhi pa/ dar dkar gyi nyag stengs na mar brkyang la bzhag go/ ngos cig ni mar
32b3(di): bya gshibs la dar dkar gyis nyag brkyangs la gzhag go/ gling bzhi bcas nas der sman bshos bdun byas la ri rab kyi steng du bzhag/ de'i steng du btsun mo gu zu can bdun
32b4(di): steng du bzhag go/ ngar phye la sha ba yu mo bdun byas la dar mang pos brgyan/ nam mkha' dkar mo g.yu'i go chu can bdun bdun la ras ma dkar mo dang / gong mo'i sgro dang
32b5(di): sna tshogs kyis brgyan no// 'phang bdun la gser ga yu'i me long can sna tshogs kyis brgyan la gzugs so// de nas yas rtags ru la ston la/ spos dang / me
32b6(di): dang 'brang rgyas bdun dang / phud gtsang mas rin chen snod bltams la bzhag/ mda' bya rgod ma la dar dkar gyi gleng bu btags la/ bu mo gtsang ma g.yo ba
32b7(di): tu gzhug go/ lag pa g.yon du me long bskur/ spos chus bu mo'i lus bkru/ ra sa gtsang ma 'am/ phying pa gtsang ma la gser g.yus phrag pa g.yas g.yon brgyan
33a1(di): pa bskon no// de nas kyir gzugs zin tsam na phud gtor bya/ lug dang yas stegs g.ya' ri dang gangs ril bab+hU 'o//
33a2(di): nam mkha'i khams kyi dkyil 'khor nas// rnam sman dkar mo rdo rje yang dag dpal// rnam sman mched bdun spyan 'dren no// dar dkar sle'u yi g.yab 'dor ro//
33a3(di): dri zhim spos kyi na bun gtibs// gsal ba'i me long mda' bzang bya rgod rten// rin chen mdos mchog 'di la spyan 'dren na// gnam sman mched bdun gshegs su
33a4(di): gsol// ga na ma sman dkar mo rdo rje yang dag dpal// sku ni 'dod chags ldem pa la// na bza' sbyin dkar go zu gsol// mtha' ma gser gyi kha chags can//

33b6(di): gsu bsnyan yang di ri ri// sha sgo kyus dang ni brengs sa brangs// sman lug dkar mo yang 'ba' dang di ri ri// nam mkha' mtho lding yang bkra dang sa sigs se sigs//

49b1(di): ru blug/ de nas thal bas kha bcad do// phur bu cig dpral ba'i dbyes su gdab/ cig snying kha ra gdab/ cig lte ba la gdab/ cig gsang sgor gdab/ kha ru spang

50a1(di): byung na sna sgo g.yas g.yon gyi steng du'o// snying la byung na mig rtsa dgod/ brang gi ze mo g.yas g.yon gzhag sha 'dar spu ldog pas sngags drag

50b1(di): gi phur bu sor bzhi pa la snying po shog chung ma bris pa sngags gong du khri tsho gcig bzlas la/ phyogs bzhi dbus dang lnga ru gzugs/ tho brtsigs nyungs kar la sngags mang po

50b7(di): gdags pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// // de nas ma mo rnams ni las las grub pas/ de la 'dul ba'i thabs ji ltar bya zhes dgongs pas/ g.yung

52b1(di): dog sna tshogs kyis// srid pa'i rgyal mo chen mo 'dis// dbyings kyi yum drug bskyed pa las// rtag pa'i rgyal mo drug tu snang // de nas srid pa'i bde 'gro gtso mo yis//

56a3(di): snying // g.yon pas 'jig rten na dbang che ba thams cad kyi rtse gnan pa/ gsang ba'i mkhar ge sar gyi dbus nas snang srid thams cad 'phel 'grib mdzad pa/ ye shes rang rig

192b2(di): la phyag 'tshal bstod// phra ma'i skyon spangs mi phyed 'khor dang ldan// nyid la rnam par 'dud pa'i 'khor gyis bskor// lha dang lha min bden pas 'dul mdzad la// nga rgyal khengs

199a3(di): snga shad g.yas pa bdud kyi khram bam ni// dam tshig nyams pa khram la 'debs pa'i rtags// phyi shad nad kyi rkyal pa btags pa ni// bstan pa 'di la gnod pa'i dgra bo la//
199a4(di): nad kyi 'debs shing dkyil 'khor bsgyur ba'i rtags// don dam bdud kyi rtags su zhag gi zo ras btang // thugs rje chags pa'i rtags su rak+ta'i thig las brgyan// 'du byed 'phran
